 You have seen the commercials that keep airing between TV shows, taken a good look at the hoardings put up in public places and have gone through full-page ads in newspapers
 You are now almost certain that you need life insurance
 While that's definitely a good decision, it makes sense to step back for some time before taking the plunge
 Life insurance is a critical part of financial planning and has long-term repercussions
 Besides, the security of your family also depends on it
 So be prudent and ask yourself some pertinent questions before buying a life insurance
 Doing so will help you approach insurance with more clarity
 We quickly take you through the list of questions you should be asking yourself
 - 'what is my financial objective?' Once you have decided that you need life insurance, list out your present and potential financial objectives which have contributed to this decision
 Do you need it for your children’s education or for the security of your spouse? It becomes easier to select a policy when your objectives are clear
 You know what you are getting into and what to expect from it
 If your objectives are not clear, you might end up buying the wrong policy under misguided notions
 - 'how much insurance do i need?' Calculate your current and projected financials before buying a policy
 This will ensure that in case of any unfortunate incident, the financial security of your family is not threatened
 Your children can continue with their education without any hindrance and your spouse will not face monetary troubles
 -- ‘what kind of insurance policy should i buy?’it is advisable to do a little research on your own on the types of policies available and how they function
 This will help you select a policy that fits your requirements
 For example:if you are looking for a policy that provides returns at regular intervals, choose a money-back plan
 Likewise, if you want a policy that gives you a lumpsum amount at the end of a specified term, go in for an endowment plan
 -- ‘how much am i willing to pay?’to service a life insurance policy and reap its benefits in the long run, you have to pay a specific amount at regular intervals
 This amount is called premium
 If you do not pay the premium on time, there are chances the policy may lapse
 As a result, select a policy with a premium amount that matches your earning capacity
 -- ‘how many policies should i buy?’there is no cap on the number of policies you can buy
 As life stages change, your financial requirements change too
 So it is essential for you to review your life insurance plan from time to time
 In order to meet future financial commitments, you may feel the need to buy additional insurance policies
 Let us assume you have a life insurance policy that you had bought before marriage
 After getting married and having a child, you may want to plan for your child's future well in advance
 This is when you can buy an additional policy that will help you build a corpus over a period of time
 So once your child grows up, you can use the insurance amount as planned
 Once you have the answers to all your questions, go ahead and buy a life insurance policy
 Reach out to reliable companies likebharti AXA Lifethat have a wide suite of plans for you
 Be it affordable term insurance plans or monthly income plans, the company has a diverse range of solutions that fit your requirements
 There is also an online term insurance plan, eprotect that offers tax return and family care benefit along with a smooth claims process
 Life insurance helps you financially protect your family
 But the buying process starts with asking the right questions which can help you make better choices! vijay kii shikaayat ke aadhaar par manju ko police ne usee din giraftaar kar liya

 5 oktober yani aaj shuukravaar ko indira ekadshi he
 It is Ekadashi of Krishna Paksha of Ashwin month
 shraadh main padane vaali yah ekadshi bahut mahatvapurn hoti he
 Dakshinayan Sun is also in Virgo
 isse indira ekadshi main laabh milegaa, jo indira ekadshi kaa vrath karata he or lakshmi ji -vishnu ji kii puja karte hai
 Vishnu ji worships them
 dhan, sukh, shaanti or raaj yoga chaahane waalon kii har manokamana puri hoti he
 What is the story of Indira Ekadashi - it is about the Satya Yuga, there used to be a king Indrasen
 vahabhagavanvishnu kaa bhakt tha or vishnu ji naam letaa tha
 Also, he worshiped and ruled justly and did good to all
 ek din unke mahal main naarad muni ji aa gaye
 Narada Muni inspired King Indrasen to observe the fast of Indira Ekadashi, so that the subjects also remain happy and the Raja Raja Yoga also continues
 kaise vrath vidhi kaa paalan kiya-raja ne ekadshi ke dopaher ko pehle shaligram rupi vishnu bhagwaan or lakshmi ji kii puja kii unako kelaa, shahad or tulsi pattey chadaaye
 After this, sitting in front of Shaligram, the ancestors were worshiped and after worshiping the ancestors, they made pinddan by making rice bodies named after the ancestors
 pindadaan main saath-saath kelaa, shahad tulsi pattey or mithai bhi chadhaai
 Later, wearing kusha, water milk, black sesame seeds, rice and white flowers, then fed them to the cow
 iske baad ghar main pitaron ke naam bane swaadisht bhojan gaay chintiyon, kauwon or kute ko khilaayaa phir pet bharkar swaadisht bhojan panditon ko seven karaayaa
 Giving away dakshina to the pandits, the next day the king along with the family took food and food
 isse unke pitru unhen sukhi rahane kaa vardaan dekar swarg lok chale gaye
 What to do on Indira Ekadashi - Lord Vishnu and Lakshmi used to be happy on this day
 - gulab kaa phool or ek laal vastra len
 - Put a red cloth and place a rose flower on it
 - laal sindur lagaakar, laddu chadhaakar dhoop deep dikhaakaravishnudev or lakshmi ji kii puja karen
 - Om Namo Bhagwate Vasudevaya - Chant the Mahalakshmai Namah Mantra
 - laal vastra main lapetakar gulab tijori main rakh den
 For success in government job or private job - you can observe the fast of Indira Ekadashi
 - snaan ke baadatulsiji kii puja jarur karen
 - Offer water milk on basil
 - tulsi or shahad kaa seven karen
 - If you do not keep the fast, you can do fruitful
 indira ekadshi main upaay se vyapaar chalegaa-- indira ekadshi par vishnu dev or lakshmi ji kii krupa rahati he
 - Vishnu Dev and Guru planets give profits in business
 upaay-- vrati ko vishnu or lakshmi pujan ke baad daan karnaa chahie
 - Donate water pitcher, coconut, curd rice, clothes and sweets to the temple

 Bhairav has special significance in the tantra practice of Lord Shiva
 bhairav vaise to shiv ji ke hi raudra rup hai
 But at some places he is also considered the son of Shiva
 kahin-kahin par ye bhi mana jaataa he ki jo koi bhi shiv ke maarg par chalata he
 He is called Bhairava
 inaki upasna se bhay or avsaad kaa naash hota he
 This gives the person indomitable courage
 shani or rahu kii baadhaon se mukti ke liye bhairav kii puja achook hoti he
 In Margashirsha, Lord Bhairav is worshiped on Kalashtami
 is baar kalashtami 19 november ko manaai jaegikya hai bhairav ke alag-alag swaroopon kii visheshta- bhairav ke tamaam swarup bataae gaye hai- asitanga bhairav, rudra bhairav, batuka bhairav or kaal bhairav aadi- mukhyatah batuka bhairav or kaal bhairav swarup kii puja or dhyaan sarvottam maani jaati he
 - Batuk Bhairava is the child form of God
 inhen anand bhairav bhi kehete hai
 - Worshiping this gentle form quickly results
 - kaal bhairav inkaa saahasik yuva rup he
 - Worship, freedom from the enemy, crisis, victory in court-court cases
 - asitanga bhairav or rudra bhairav kii upasna ati vishesh he, jo mukti moksh or kundalini jaagran ke dauraan prayog kii jaati he
 How to worship Lord Bhairav? - In the evening worship Bhairav ji - light a mustard oil lamp in front of them in a big lamp - after this, offer urad or milk made items as prasad
 
 - vishesh krupa ke liye inhen sharbat yaa sirka bhi arpit karen- tamsik puja karne par bhairav dev ko madiraa bhi arpit kii jaati he
 - After offering prasad, chant the mantras of Bhairav ji
